申報醫藥周刊傷寒發揮五（中）（太陽下）  余雲岫　　與結胸相似者，爲痞，傷寒論曰：「脈浮而緊，而復下之，緊反入裏，則作痞，按之自濡，但氣痞耳。」方中行注曰：「濡，言不硬不痛而柔軟也」，按方說是也，管子幼官篇，「藏溫濤」，注日，一君之月癖者，溫和濡緩」，是濡可訓軟，又集韵二十八獨，有輭軟通濡，是濡卽軟字矣，柯韵伯改濡作硬，徐靈胎，訓濡爲濕，皆非是，傷寒論又曰，「心下痞，按之濡」，又曰，「但滿而不痛者，此爲痞」總諸條觀之，傷寒論之痞，乃傷寒鼓腸證而不甚者也，若鼓腸之甚者，按之亦不較，其危險亦大，所謂臟結者，或卽此乎？　　結胸之後，所當注意者，熱入血室也，傷寒論熱入血室，凡有三條日，「婦入中風，發熱惡寒，經水適來，得之七八日，熱除而脈遲，身凉，脑脇下滿，如結胸狀，囈語者，此爲熱入血室也」。又曰「婦人中風七八日，續得寒熱發作有時，經水滴斷者，此爲熱入血室，其血必結，故使如癥狀，發作有時」。又曰，「婦人傷寒發熱，經水適來，畫日明了，暮則囈語，如見鬼狀者，此爲熱入血室，無犯胃氣及上二焦，必自愈」，欲論此候，當先决定血室之果爲何物，成聊攝明理諭，以爲血室卽衝脈，方喻諸家，從而和之，柯韻伯以爲是肝，徐靈胎以爲是心肝兩臟，皆以意爲說，而無明確之蹬據，陳自明婦人良方，以爲是胞門子戶，羅謙甫衛生寶鑑，屬爲是女子胞，程式醫彀，以爲是子宮，張景岳三焦命門辨，亦以爲是子戶，為金匱要略，婦人雜病二十二，有曰，一婦人少腹滿，如敦狀，小便微難，而不渴，生後者，此爲水與血俱結在血室也，大黃甘遂湯主之」。然則傷寒論所謂「胸脇下滿，如結胸狀」者，乃在少腹也，少腹者，膀胱子宮之所在也，子宮有病，其影響往往及於膀胱，故曰，「小便微難」也，以此論之，陳羅程張四子之說，較爲有據矣，且獨見諸婦人，又獨見諸婦人月經之時及生產之後，其爲子宮，更可無疑，由此觀之，所謂熱入血室者，小骨盤腹膜炎也，子宮周圍炎也，其劇者，亦能生腦膜炎，故囈語，而神經衰弱之女子，每至經行之期，神經證候更甚，故見鬼也，其輕者能自愈，故曰「無犯胃氣及上二焦，必自愈」，如瘧狀，發作有時者，化膿熱也。余嘗診一左姓女子，經來中止，發熱，少腹脹痛不可近，送至同德醫院，此時長院者爲龐京周先生，以其爲處子也，不欲遽檢查其生殖器，姑以泥膏敷其少腹，以觀其經過。至入院之第三日，突然有白色之膿，大最從陰道出，自是病候頓减，無幾日，全愈而退院矣。此乃局限性少腹部化膿症，（或卽盲腸周圍局限性膿瘍），自陰道破潰而出者也，此亦熱入血室之例也。然病不在子宮內，無所謂血室，謂之熱入血室者，古人想像懸擬之辭，今則不宜用矣。今世醫家，但見婦女熱病有囈語者，不問其少腹有無滿硬，方案上多書熱入血室字樣，可謂不思之甚矣，想像懸擬之辭，其流弊如此也。　　傷寒論曰：「傷寒脈結代，心動悸，炙甘草湯主之」，又曰，「脈，按之來緩，而時一止，復來者，名曰結，又，脈來動而中止，更來小數，中有還者，反動，名曰結陰也，脈來動而中止，不能自還，因而復動，名曰代陰也，得此脈者，必難治」。按結代等脈，拙著皇漢醫學批評，已論之矣，若以較嚴格言之，結代脈者，卽新醫之不規則脈中之期外收縮Extrasystole及房室刺戟傳達障碍也。何謂期外收縮，何謂房室刺戟傳達障碍，非明心臟刺戟傳達之生理不可，今請略言之：疾病常識問答  程瀚章　　（六十六）慢性和結核性腹膜炎　　（問）什麽叫做慢性腹膜炎？　　（答）普通很少，大都從急性腹膜炎遷延而成：或因外傷腹水穿刺或腸潰瘍而起初就成慢性的。　　（問）什麽叫做結核性腹膜炎？　　（答）結核性腹膜炎，也是慢性腹膜炎的一種，由於結核菌侵犯腹膜而起。大都續發於他部的結核病，像肺癆，骨膜結核，結核性肋膜炎等。　　（問）這兩種腹膜炎，病狀怎樣？　　（答）慢性單純性腹膜炎和結核性腹膜炎病狀相同，都是潛行性發病，或突然發病的。　　（問）病人是否和急性腹膜炎一樣訴腹痛？　　（答）並不很痛。祇有輕微的壓痛。腹部中等度膨滿，但並非全腹部都起膨滿。間或有腹壁扁平陷凹緊張。　　（問）觸診的時候，覺得怎樣？　　（答）觸診的時候，見有限局性抵抗，或瘤狀隆起；這是因爲大綱膜或腸間膜腺腫脹的緣故。　　（問）腹膜腔內，也有滲出液體嗎？　　（答）有的；但量不很多。而滲出液常限留於一部，所以不像腹水那樣跟着體位而流動的。　　（問）病人的身體有無發熱？　　（答）有時有發熱的。　　（問）還有其他病狀嗎？　　（答）還有嘔吐吃逆等病狀。　　（問）單純性慢性和結核性的腹膜炎的區別，應該怎樣診斷？　　（答）祇要考查病人的旣往史，有無消耗性發熱。而結核性的滲出液，富於淋巴球，又帶血性，又結核性的腹膜炎，缺乏腹痛。　　（問）這兩種腹膜炎的預斷吉兇怎樣？　　（答）非結核性腹膜炎，預後比較佳良，有時可以治愈。結核性的，大多數是危險的。但比較他部分的結核症，却有一綫希望。　　（問）單純性慢性和結核性的腹膜炎，療法怎樣？　　（答）第一，要注意食物的衛生，多吃營物質豐富的食物。第二，腹部用酒精濕布溫濕布，或塗灰白較膏，木焦油洋橄油，沃替盎油膏。或用人工太陽燈照射。第三，內服藥，祇有用帮助吸收或减少滲出的藥品像碘劑或松溜滽製劑。　　（問）有行開腹衛的必要嗎？　　（答）結核性腹膜炎，有行開腹放水，而治愈的。又放出水分後注入消毒的空氣（六〇〇—一〇〇〇立方緾）有偉效。高血壓與血管硬化（上）  月祺　　——醫學故事之九——　　血高壓與血管硬化，不一定是同一事情。二者都是人體隨年齡衰老的自然法則。在高血壓的例子中，或許有硬化血管存在着——至少是最小血管起硬化。但外端血管的硬化不一定與血壓的增高相伴隨。而且，外端血管——如在手腕及前額等處——起硬化的人們，可以活到長壽的年齡。　　高血壓本身，種類不同。伏耳哈（Volhard）和發爾（Fahr）曾寫過一篇著名的論文，把高血壓分爲「良意」的與「惡意」的二類。這確實是一種頗有見地的分類。　　固然，測量血壓成爲醫界的一種普通察騐方法，只是三十年來的事，但血壓問題的討論却是於二百年前開始的。一七三三年，一個英國牧師，名叫海耳斯（Stephen　Hales）的曾用一種很簡單的方法測騐馬的血壓。他拿一技九呎長的玻璃管挿入那馬的股血管。他發見血液在玻璃管內昇高八呎三吋，這表示血液所受的壓力足够支持這樣高的一段血液。目前用以測量人體血壓的頗類於此的器具，大槪於一八五零年開始被若干生理學家所採用，但應用的塲所只限於生理學實騐室中。到了一九零五年，從測騐人體血壓所得的充分的材料，使幾家人壽保險公司認爲這測騐血壓的方法對於他們頗有用處。從那時起，數百萬人的血壓，壽命，及死後察看內部器官的情形，一一被詳細地留記下來，從此一般醫生獲得藉以研究血壓問題的大量的資料。　　如前所述，血壓是與年齡俱進的。爲什麽呢？因爲在年靑的時候，血管是彈性的，但當人體逐漸衰老的時候，血管的彈性組織漸被織維組織和石灰鹽所代替，因此它們就逐漸變得僵硬。我們知道，自來水通過橡皮管的壓力比通過鐵管的壓力低，這是因爲有彈性的橡皮管會帮助着擠下在裏面通過的水的綠故。血管硬化影響血壓，正和這情形相同。這是對於高血壓的「機械的」解釋。　　此項「機械的解釋」曾受各方面的批評。至少一般醫生界對此並不一致贊成。現在，讓我把他們的反對論和他們自己的見解列舉於下，并論述其是否具有充分的理由。　　對於「機械的解釋」的最有力的反對論，根據於注重兩個事實：（一）在許多例子，易於察看的血管——如在手腕和籲籲等部分——確起顯著的硬化，但用水銀測量血壓器測量血壓却不見昇高；（二）在若干極度高血壓的例子，同樣的血管並不顯明地增厚。可是，在長遠以前，名叫健威（Janeway）的學者曾努力於使這些顯然相反的事實不致衝突。他指明：在外端血管起硬化的同一時間，內部的大血管——如總動脈及其枝脈——仍然可以照舊富於彈性，而造成變化的主因所在正是這些大血管。　　血管硬化是一種情狀，這情狀影響血管的情形隨部分而不同，有時造成血腰的昇高，有時則否。　　另一個對於「機械的解釋」的反對論是這樣：在某種極度的例子，血壓昇得非常高，但死後用顯微鏡察看血管膜，却毫無變化。從生理學實騐室中發生的

Page 20

情形得來的解釋，可以用作對於這些例子的解釋。生理學告訴我們，血管的衣膜含有一種肌肉組織；又，某種神經的刺戟，會造成這些肌肉的收縮，使血管更小更僵硬。這些馬達神經的刺戟，可藉某種藥物或化學物質的溶液加入血液中造成。所以，這是可能的，就是：某種物質留在血液中，造成連續的血管收縮，同時却不至於造成可藉顯微鏡看到的恒久的變化。無論如何，這些嚴重型式的存生，已使敏銳的觀察者——卽伏爾哈與發爾二人——宣稱高血壓可分二類，而他們給予這二類高血壓的名稱魷是「良意的」與「惡意的」。無錫新醫藥衛生概況  過醒虎　　無錫是中國模範縣治，位於京滬鐵路中心，交通便利，水路有大運河，陸路有京滬鐵路，近年來又先後興築錫澄鍚宜錫滬三大公路，錫澄路從無錫到江陰，錫宜路從無錫到宜興，錫滬路從無錫到上海，中間經過常熟太倉嘉定而達上海，縣內的鄉鎭公路，也很發達，倘從錫宜路到宜興，便能和京杭國道相接，可見無錫和南京杭州間的交通，也很便利。　　無錫衛生行政，由公安局辦理，每年舉行衛生運動，收買蒼蠅，貼衛生標語，勸導食品店，加蓋紗罩，每年暑期，由縣府撥欺，舉辦臨時防疫醫院，勸導人民免費注射預防霍亂疫苗，尙有各鄉鎭慈善家，舉辦施診給藥局，中醫公會亦舉辦施診給藥局，由會員義務担任，無鍚民衆對於公共衛生，素不注意，街道骯髒，坑厠齷齪，河水混濁，使蛟蟲病菌蕃殖，故每屆暑天，患霍亂瘧疾者很多，城中雖有淸道夫和淸河夫，並改良坑厠，但市民對於公共衛生，仍不注意。　　無錫監獄，平日飲食起居，不很衛生，自新監落成後，遂逐漸改良，但分駐所，及看守所，一仍其舊，入夏以來，天氣炎熱，近數日氣溫總在百度左右，羈押人犯，人數擁擠，聚居一室，汗氣薰蒸，酷熱相逼，疫癘流行，每多突然中暑而病者。　　無錫有醫院已近三十年，最初創辦的，是美國聖公會開的普仁醫院，創辦在光緒三十四年二月，院長美國人李克樂，很得地方人士信仰，院內設備完善，分內外各科，有病床六十張，職員醫師三十多人，是無錫最早最著名最完備的醫院，無錫除省立平民產院，民衆醫院外，沒有大規模的公立醫院，便利一般窮苦的病人求醫，自國府厲行禁毒以來，無錫設立縣戒姻所，經費由省府撥充，人員也是由省委派，所址設在從前之遷善局，後改勞工醫院，由勞工醫院停辦後，卽改設今之縣戒姻所，設備尙佳，可容姻犯一百二十人，辦理尙好，無錫半慈善醫院，由紅卐字會助資創設之能仁醫院，院長衛質文醫師，設備甚佳，取費較私人醫院爲廉，無錫私人開設的醫院很多，但取費很貴。　　無錫有醫師公會，及中華西醫公會無錫分會，共有新醫醫師一百人左右，已向衛生署登記者，七十餘人，於十八年前已經開業，與衛生署所頒之變通給蹬查格符合，因消息滯呆，錯過登記者二十餘人，現由無錫西醫公會，赴省請願，發給開業執照，據聞頗有希望，以九十四萬一千三百七十二人之人口計算，每九千四百十三人中有一新醫師。　　無錫藥房，資本較大，設備稍週者，有五洲藥房，大陸藥房，太和藥房，中法藥房等，惟尙無藥劑師配方，其他藥房，如中和藥房，中外藥房，興昌藥房，中西藥房，中南藥房，大英藥房，華美藥房，兄弟藥房，專門經售成藥及化妝品，略備少數原藥，兼及其他營業。耳鼻喉眼衛生常識  唐仁縉　　（六十二）　發聲器　　所謂發聲器者，魷是屬於呼吸器中的喉頭。喉頭的形狀。彿彷漏斗。是由三個無對的軟骨及三個有對的軟骨互相疊述而成此形。無對的軟骨。就是環狀軟骨·甲狀軟骨·及會厥軟骨。有對的軟骨。就是披裂軟骨·小角軟骨·及楔狀軟骨。這等軟骨再由喉頭靱帶及喉頭肌肉彼此繫述。更從牠們的共同作用。而營發聲的機能有發聲機能的主要部。就是聲帶。聲帶位於喉頭的中央。是一對具有彈力性的靱帶。在兩聲帶間所有的空隙。稱爲聲門。我們在呼吸的時候。聲門立卽哆開。變爲三角形，（參照下列A圖）。發聲的時候。聲門立卽合閉。變爲柳葉狀（參列下列B圖）。聲門的能開能閉。是乃喉頭肌肉運動的結果。聲音的可以發生。是由聲門合閉呼出空氣的時候。緊張的聲帶。爲氣流所襲突而振動所致。聲帶的長短及弛張。與聲音的高低。很有關係。所以一般女子及十五歲以下男兒的聲調。高而細。且柔軟（無怪乎悅耳動聽）。成年男子的聲調。低而粗。這就是因爲女子的聲帶短細緊張的緣故。我國一般俗間的流言。謂從聲調的高低粗細。可以辨別是否童子一層。無非也就是根據方才講過的生理變化而言。　　此外尙須注意的。就是我們言語的時侯。並非單獨倚賴發聲器的喉頭。蓋空氣通過聲門的時候。必須附有咽腔，口腔，軟口蓋，舌，齒，口唇，下顎骨，及鼻腔的共同運動作用。方始可以成爲言語。假使一旦某部發生變化。失去作用。那就立卽感覺言語困難。或竟不能言語。所以在咽頭實扶的里，扁桃腺病，口腔炎，軟口蓋破裂，舌炎，齒牙脫落，口唇缺裂（兎唇），下顆骨脫臼，肥原性鼻炎，及鼻茸腫等等時候。常常威覺到言語困難的痛苦。這是很明瞭的事實。　　如果聲音一旦發生嘶嘎（就是聲啞）。大都就是聲帶發生變化的明證。牠的變化的原因，很多。據我的經騐看起來。大槪不出喉頭炎，喉頭實扶的里，喉頭結核，喉頭梅毒，喉頭腫瘍，迥歸神經麻痺，及歌人結節的幾種。關於這幾種的詳細病情。大半已經在本刊發表過。讀者諸位。當可回憶。　　（附）發聲器的衛生若有嘶嗄。應卽嚴守（一）禁止談話，（二）多吸新鮮空氣，（三）避免乾燥寒冷不潔的空氣。（四）室內最好有散佈水蒸氣的裝置（可使空氣濕潤），（四）烟酒及辛辣的食物，能刺戟喉頭粘膜，避之爲宜，及（六）速就專科醫師檢查喉頭等等六條（Ａ）呼吸時保聲門悤開（Ｂ）發聲時保聲門合閉現代花柳病學通俗演講（十六）  陳生白（編述）殷木强（校正）　　丁·治療及預防　軟性下疳患者。當保守身體之安靜。禁止長途步行及劇烈運動。避絕情慾之亢奮及刺戟品之飲用。以免病原菌之蔓延。而速潰瘍之治瘉。在局部如防腐，消毒及洗滌之外用。在全身如自家血淸，蛋白製劑及Vaccin之注射等。可隨症施治。各擇其宜。　　其預防。略如一般性病預防法。　　第二章　關於軟性下疳性淋巴管炎及淋巴腺炎　　甲·淋巴管炎軟性下疳之經過中。屢侵陰莖背面之淋巴管。惹起淋巴管炎。淋巴管作疼痛性索狀腫賬。該部皮膚潮紅。漸乃軟化，破潰，排膿，作下疳樣潰瘍。　　乙·淋巴腺炎鼠蹊部淋巴腺之腫脹（卽橫痃）。亦爲軟性下疳時常見之合併症。此時以生理上陰部淋巴交叉行走之故。每在漬瘍之反對側。見鼠蹊淋巴腺之腫脹。當腫脹之初。覺行動時之牽引感。次覺疼痛。步履維艱。及其長大。或如鳩卵。或如雞卵或更大。該部皮膚漸亦潮紅，浮腫，化膿。並伴有高度之發熱及全身症狀。　　至於預防及治療。卽保守安靜，罨包濕布，塗佈軟膏，照射X光綫，注射Vaccin與蛋白刺戟劑及切開排膿。或避免病毒之蔓延，或促進膿汁之吸收，或增加體內之抵抗力，及殺菌，排毒以作根本之企圖等等。如應用適當。每能預防本病之發生或速其治瘉也。　　第四編　鼠蹊淋巴肉芽腫　　鼠蹊淋巴肉芽職（Lymphogranuloma　inguinale）徵諸旣往文獻。與此類似之記載。雖屬不尠。但確鑿與性交有關之報告。則爲一九一三年一月法人Nicolas，Favre，Durand是。本病之病原菌。尙未發見。現假定爲一種濾過性病原體。因其由性交而傳染。又稱之曰第四種性病。本病之傳佈於國內者。亦數見不鮮。惜尙未能引起一般之注意爲遺憾耳　　甲·症狀本病之感染。因性交爲媒介。已無可疑。故多犯靑年男女。而尤其男子爲多。其症狀有　　一·原發疹本症潛伏期尙不明。大約感染以後。經一二週至數月之潛伏期。於龜頭或包皮內板起表皮剝落。形成小潰瘍，小水泡或丘疹。以無顯著之自覺症狀。患者疲憊略不知魷醫。止痛的醫學（三〇）  李興　　科學醫旣日有進步，當然不能置歸女的疼痛於不顧。現在已有的止痛方法是於生產痛時可注射少量麻醉品以止痛，或內服少量鎭痛藥也可，但於胎兒落牠前約兩小時以內，不宜注射麻醉品，以免胎兒落地後悶氣。於胎兒落地前痛極時，產婦可於每次痛來時吸蒙藥，但蒙藥不宜過量，以免生產作用停止。如果是難產須施行手術，助以局部麻藥或蒙藥。　　急性輸卵管炎　　男性淋病傳染，旣有突飛猛進之勢，女性也當然不能倖免。女性淋病之多少是與男性之淋病成正比例。女性所發生的淋病是與男性的完全相同，同爲一種雙球菌，所以男性可以傳染女性，女性也可以傳染男性，如此循環不已。女的得了淋病起初發炎在陰道部，發炎漸漸向內達到子宮頸。有時機會好或治療得當毛病達到此處可漸砌全愈。但有人不楚這樣僥倖，疾病達到子宮頸再向上經過子宮內腔達到兩輸卵管（兩輸卵管位於小腹內自子宮兩上角起向兩旁伸出各約三寸左右長短）。淋病一達到了輸卵管就成了淋病之內病，普通藥洗與內服藥都達不到了。　　無病的輸卵管大小略小於鉛筆，但一發炎了就腫脹直徑常達一寸餘。管內生出大量膿水，管壁也增厚，發紅發腫。由於這種的變化患者第一種的感覺是嚴重的痛。痛是在小腹內卽骨盆內，下腹兩旁都痛，同時身體也發冷發熱，下部排洩也加多。患者食慾也隨之减退，身體平素不肥胖的，就不免漸顯消瘦，就是肥胖的身體也必軟弱。如此經數星期之久，病勢减輕或漸全愈。後來如果再受一次傳染這種毛病也可照樣發作。若是時發時止，久之便成了慢性輸卵管炎。　　治療這種毛病與治療別種急性發炎原理相同。第一急務卽臥床靜心休息。休息是任何急性發炎病的基本治法，也是止痛術的要素。痛的部分若是動來動去不使休息自然是更痛。若是休息了疼痛可以减少，發炎也可漸漸停止。第二種辦法是用熱療止痛，如用熟濕熱敷於下腹一日多次。最近有用人工發熱法治療頗有驚人效騐，法卽用生熱電機或熱水涔將病者身體溫度增高到一百零五度（平常體溫爲九十八度零十分之六度）每次歷四五小時之久。由實騐和淋病菌不能抵抗一百零四度以上熟度根久。如果由一次或數次之人工發熱將淋病菌殺死，病自全愈。一次或多次人工發熱治療確可治愈急性輸卵管炎。此法用於男性淋病亦有同樣效果。此種方法須由有經騐醫師負責實行。　　還有一種方法卽注射反應作用蛋白質，如消毒去脂牛乳，淋菌或別種細菌苗漿，使身體起反應作用以增加身體抵抗淋菌之力。　　外科手術痛　　在中古時代已不斷有人施行外科手術，但從中古時代到十九世紀之初外科學並沒有進步。其不發達之原因爲不明細菌學。沒有病菌學的知識施行外科手術是一種危險的事，也是一種投機的手術。一直等到十九世紀的當中才有英屬之外科鼻祖李斯特氏起來提倡滅菌外科手術。明白了細菌與疾病之因果關係與消滅病菌之方法外科學與外科手術才有一日千里之進步。　　外科學之進步也，爲科學醫開一頁新記錄。有的從前要死的病現在有了辦法，從前無治的病現在有治了。外科學之有造於人類實屬不小。　　助外科手術發達的第一是細菌學，第二是止痛藥物，例如蒙藥，局部麻藥，麻醉藥，鎭靜神經藥等等。使患者於施行手術前神經鎭靜或麻木，不驚不撓，施行手術時有各種麻藥，或局部麻藥，使病人不知痛苦。於施行手術後正當使用麻醉藥使患者神志昏迷而不知有痛苦。現在全世界醫學界仍是繼續研究新方法以減少人類之痛苦。　　外科手術於近數十年也傳到了我國。我國人起初是很怕痛的，過有外科病時往往說「怕痛怕痛」以求避免外科手術。此爲人之常情誰也不能以爲怪。就是一年到頭開人家刀的外科專家到了自己有了毛病假設有法避免外科手術他也未嘗不避免。就是一年到頭拔人家牙的牙科專家他有了牙病個設施避免拔去自己牙他也未必去拔掉自己牙。在患者無可避免手術時外科家如果看人家所患的病如同自己患的一樣，施行外科適當的手術，將樂於施行在自己身上施行在病人身上，患者宜服從這種外科翳師的指導。這是理想的外科家也是任何國家所需要的。要知外科手術可否避免須確切明白病理。確知了病理才可以知道避免外科手術是否有益。確知了避免外科手術有極大的危險，萬不可避免，也萬不可怕外科手術痛一定要避免。須知愚昧的避免外科手術輕則要多受痛苦，重則要發生性命危險。例如，身上長一瘤於大如蠶豆時，怕痛不要割去，等到後來瘤長到十磅或二十磅重時必須割去才割去，痛苦當然要加增千百倍。再如，胃瘡穿破如果愚昧避免外科手術患者將無生活希望。故遇有外科病症時醫病兩方預先作精密的考盧而後施行適當的治療法不但可减少痛苦並且還可保有生命的安全。消息　　醫訟案件彙抄預約截止　中華醫學會業務保障委員會宋國賓醫師編輯之醫藝案件彙抄第一集，爲數年來國內醫病糾紛案件之總集。包含醫案二十餘伴。凡兩造之訟狀。法院之判詞。以及醫學機關之鑑定文件。靡不羅列。全書約三十餘萬言。佔四百餘頁之獲。自發售預約以來。各地訂購者日有多起。至八月三十一日止。已有數千餘戶。現該書預約期已滿。存盡祗數百冊。如欲購者須照實價一元。不折不扣。並聞該書購者以醫師律師法官佔最多數云。

申報本埠增刊談言本市各機關實行三化生活  夢若　　頃上海市新運促進會，以實行新生活，應以各機關爲先，愛依總會所頒「生活軍事化，生產化，藝術化初步推行方案，」制訂「上海市各機關實行三化生活初步方案，」分發市內各國立市立機關，轉發各公務人貝，以資實行。聞所訂方案，係採由淺入深方法，分期施行。其第一期要點包括三項原則：（一）使養成迅速整齊之行動，（二）使養成勞動節約之生活，（三）使養成有禮守法之習慣。此要點以二個月爲一期，自九月一日起實行，由各該機關長官負督促推行之責。在實行期間，新運會得隨時派員查察。　　新生活運動，自開始實行迄今，雖爲期祇有年餘，但因全國各方合力推行，的結果，成績亦頗不差。單以本市而言，新生活十名詞，已爲婦孺皆知，市上自經新生活運動服務隊努力活動，市容已爲之一變，各公共塲所，亦頗見秩序齊盛，黃包車夫雖在熟日下奔馳，鈕扣亦不敢放開。此皆爲人民奉行新生活之一斑。　　此次本市新運促進會，以實行新生活，應以各機關爲先，故特制訂一實行三化生活初步方案，分發各公務人員實行。此舉於新運前途，頗多助力。蓋各機關公務人員，爲市民表率，對於新生活，若能以身作則，首先奉行。則今後於此運動的推行，當可收得良好的效果。因公務人員的一舉一動，直接間接，皆足以影響於人民也。　　我國官民之間，幾如隔一鴻溝，分成兩個不同的階級。位高祿厚者，往往窮奢極侈。或則日夜徵逐於酒色塲中，過其頹廢的生活。此種行爲，不但有阻礙個人的進取，抑亦有妨害公務的執行。故欲澄淸吏治，改善官塲的生活，實爲要圖。而改善之策，使各機關公務人員實行新生活方案，是頗適當的。　　觀第一期所訂方案，雖甚淺易，要亦公務人員日常生活所必需奉行。其中如婚喪不濫發帖，待人接物應持和靄態度，此皆爲公務人員所最缺乏的行爲和禮貌，故今後各機關公務人員，若能切實奉行此三化生活，則新運前敵眾我寡，定必有更驚人的發展。蟋蟀  譚曇　　自己做事沒有恒心，所以，無論什麽事，繼續到三年的實在不大有；只有一件事，我足足繼績了十年，那就是養蟋蟀。　　不知道十歲還是十一歲那年，我跟着仲兄在附近一個學校裏住讀。秋天，剛開學，沒有上課，我因爲第一次離開家，所以常常一個人坐在房間裏對着窗外一株沒有皮的紫薇花發呆。紫薇花又各百日紅，開花的時候極長，我天天對着他實在有一點厭了，但是沒法，窗外除了這種瑣小的紅色的花就什麽也沒有了。　　一天，我正在發呆的時侯，仲兄忽然從外邊來，手裏捧了幾只磁的器具，匆匆的放在臥牀下邊又出去了。我好奇心動就偷偷地去拿他牀下的東西弄開看看，原來每一管裏都有一頭蟋蟀。蟋蟀我本來就認識的，同時也知道牠們會鬥，這時候實在無聊得太厲害，魷揀兩隻大一，些的放在一處，讓他們鬥。果然兩隻蟋蟀鬥得極起勁，好久一隻才敗了，我就輕手輕脚的把他原舊分好盆放在牀底下。經過這次親手弄他們一鬥，我的養蟋蟀念頭就提了起來，正想找幾只管頭預備捉蟋蟀的時候，忽然紫薇花底下，幾塊斷磚中，有蟋蟀的鳴聲傳了過來，我就跑到紫薇花底下去聽一聽，原來從一塊小小的斷磚下發出。我那時非常高興，輕輕把斷磚揭開一看，見一隻灰黑色的蟋蟀，就拚命的抓去，抓到之後，我就急急跑回臥室，把仲兄牀下才鬥收的一隻倒去，把新捉到的一隻放下，把盆蓋蓋住，一回揭開一看，雄偉非常，比仲兄的幾隻神氣雄健得多，我那時就很珍重的藏好，後來仲兄回來，看了也嘖嘖稱奇，他把所有的和我那一隻鬥，也完全敗北。從此我養蟋蟀的興趣提了起來一連十年沒有間斷。　　因爲經騐的豐富，對於蟋蟀的强弱，一目了然。但當我得了一本呌做「促織經」的小書後，我的對於蟋蟀的判別力更加敏銳。「促織」是蟋蟀的別名，「促織經」是淸人著作前有名士尤同人序。對於蟋蟀的各方面論得很詳細，自然這裏是無法轉錄的；那末，下邊我還是說一點促蟋蟀的趣味罷！　　蟋蟀夜鳴，我們對於蟋蟀有經騐的人只要一聽他的鳴就知道他的强弱。所以每到秋初，我總是一吃晚飯就睡，一覺醒來正當夜半，這時候月明人靜，蟋蟀亂鳴我披衣起牀，點一紙燈籠，輕輕地跑出房來。夜風襲袂薄寒中人，我常常引起一陣陣的感傷，無從捕促，而歸房晏臥，不然就潛潛等等，屏息側耳，一則確實知道蟋蟀的所在，就做一個記號，到明日天色一明，再來捕捉，如此往往終夜。　　除了捕蟋蟀外，最有趣味的就是開鬥了。開鬥我們的術語叫「開欄」。每逢上中下三旬的三六九日爲開柵之期，遠近的蓄「蟲子」（蟲子也是術語）都携着健者趕來，先由經紀人過枰稱明了重量，然後擇重量相等者配對開鬥。博金由兩蟋蟀之主互相講定，約分三種，高爲十元以上，次爲十元以下，最少爲不滿一元者，講定之後，卽行開鬥，勝敗一分，彩聲立起，那時勝蟲的意氣揚揚，而敗者自垂頭喪氣。酒食相勞，酬酢甚忙，這種情形雖則許多又都說是「市井氣」但我樂此不疲。　　自從離開家庭，養蟋蟀之事，就間斷了。秋風一起，街頭就有蟋蟀出售，未能忘情，聊購一二頭，然目的已不在鬥，而在聽他的鳴聲了。　　「少年哀樂過於人，消息都防父老驚」，目前人事勞勞，連這種「勝業」都不能繼續，實在令人惆悵！　　宋玉九辯云：「哀蟋蟀之宵征」，歐陽永叔秋聲賦云「四壁蟲聲，唧唧，似助余之嘆息，」現在蟋蟀之於我，不過「助余嘆息」而已。浮浪人的手册  夏蔭　　（一）送行　　呷下最後一口濃味的咖啡，爵士的繁聲在耳邊消失去了。一輛白牌的汽車，裝着四個年靑的浮浪者的心，偷偷的爬過夜靜的街。跳下車，拖着倦疲的步伐，走上暗影幢幪的碼頭；夜靜的黃浦江飄過腥味的凉風，四個人都不約而同吁了一口氣；望着散綴在江面的巨船的燈火，幾疑是天邊的星點。哦，浮浪者的寂寞的行程！　　靠船邊的碼頭上，隨地躺着熟睡的襤褸羣；一些短打的同胞，許是生活剝奪了他們的睡眼，散坐在暗影裏談着我們聽不懂的事故。當甲板上的臭味術到鼻孔來時，四個人都更變得沉默了。　　茶房將朋友的手提箱接到房子裏去。客廳裏兩座小電風扇旋亮着耀目的金光，軋嗡軋嗡的發出微嚮。一切都靜止着。看看貼掛在艙壁上的大鐘，短針正指着二點二二刻。離開船還有三點鐘。　　剛才霓虹燈下的狂興消失去了，大家雖然對着話，臉上却流露出疲倦和黯然的神色。生活逼得我們分散，各爲着自己的前途奔程！流浪人送流浪人，這寂寞的行旅呀，已倦困了每個年靑的心，歲月一季一季的老去。流浪的行程可無息下的時候啦。　　甲板上正吹着習習的江風，可吹不淨心中的別離的悽楚。友情是值得惓戀的，然而今宵可要離散開去呀！倚若船欄，默默的望着夜深的黑黝黝的江面，不由自己想念到自己的浮浪生涯，前麅影事，都一齊湧上心來。我深深的向江面太息着。　　——唉，今宵是自己送着人行，以後恐怕只有自己一個寂寂寞寞的背起行裝奔趨了。　　（二）夜歸　　燈炧，人倦，夢也闌跚；咖啡的澀味淡了，再會，歡笑的假情的女兒！扔去手中的殘姻，眼底飛起一陣困感，一串寂寞的翅翼，偷偷溜進脆弱的心。

Page 23

沒有悔恨，也沒有歡欣；疲倦溶解了整個身心。默默的邁向夜靜的柏油，街燈昏昏的，照着兩隻年輕的影兒，拖着沉澀的步子，皮鞋擦出單調的嘆息，又飄散在夜靜的街心。　　一障露凉爽颯的天風飄過街空，猛抬頭望望無語的天河，正是繁月缺，舉掌摸摸冷滑的雙頰，心頭微微滲進一股酸味，唉，似水的年華，靑春已全不珍惜的浪費在慘綠的情熱中了。　　汽車向夜之郊野馳去，一程一程吞噬着死蛇一般懶睡的柏油路。心是空寂的。車窗外，星斗點點，都向後邊旋過去。懶懶的靠在車塾上，闔下眼皮，頓覺一陣輕飄，身像離了車座，我失了心力的主宰。我想放開喉嚨，用自己的無譜的歌，驅逐這沉濃的睡意和疲倦；但是，我可聽不到自己的歌聲。哦哦，這浮浪的慘綠的生涯，它已奪去我振作的生命之力了。　　在一條照着星光的石子路上，與同伴打了個無語的道別，踅進自己的睡房來；沒有扭亮燈，胡亂褪下衣裝倒在枕被凌亂的床上。這就是浮浪者的睡宿之地喲，喃喃的自語着。糢糢糊糊的，閘北工廠的笛聲飄進耳邊來……　　（三）莫問我的家　　莫問我的家，家，這已成了徒有惹人感傷的份兒了。　　飛出故巢的雛燕，只有用自己年輕的銳力去經營安宿的新巢的，故巢雖然溫暖，那已不能供牠戀就了。縱一年一度的歸去探望，那不徒然多增一番酸情嗎？　　也莫問我是否一人獨自；也莫歆羨行裝爲處的浮浪生涯。傷痛的是空支付出年少的熱情，換來一塲慘綠的糜爛；而今，寂寞已噙走了歡笑的意趣，日子空留下浮浪的詛咒：與倦厭。　　再無舊日的戀情去顧念溫暖的家。出巢的乳燕只有用自己年輕的銳力去經營安宿的新巢。我是要在浮浪的旅程中去尋求安宿自家的新巢了。播音節目國學　　馮明權「古文觀止」　　明遠（九六〇）上午七時半至八時半　　講題　莊子逍遙遊　　至理所在。可以心遇。而不可以力求。斷編殘簡。呻吟諷誦。越宿已有遺落。至於途歌里詠。偶入吾耳。則雖終身而不忘。天下之理。固眩於求而眞於遇也。理有觸於吾心。無意而直遭。無約而相會。油然自生。雖吾不能以語人。况可以力求乎。一涉於求。雖有見非其正。食用飲食之間。無非至理。惟吾迫而求之。則隨得隨失。研精極思。日入於鑿。曾不知是理交發於吾前。而吾自不遇。是非不用力之罪。乃用力之罪也。歌唱　　星星歌唱社　　新新（七八〇）下午六時至七時　　夜月之歌（白燕）睡的贊美（飛虹）鐵蹄下的歌女（朱琪）旋宮艷史（飛亞）春潮回來吧（（朱琪）（白燕）說愛就愛（飛亞）（飛虹）慈母搖籃曲（朱琪）老鳳陽歌（飛亞）　　美玲團　　航業（一一八〇）下午六時至七時　　小孩與花（前奏曲）放在心頭（靜美）小妹妹的心（黃韻）乘風飛去（賴玲）因爲你（程瑩）娘子軍歌（王佩佩）凰陽歌（程英英）愛情是什麽（黃韻）妹妹我怪你（余雪麗）蘇武牧羊（王超）摩登女郎（靜美）南海美人（黃韻）　　星光社　　富星（九二〇）下午六時三刻至七時半　　紅顏軍士（黃喋）愛的花（周璐）銀色的凄凉（競芳）女軍人（淑珍）愛情如玫瑰（王琪）小東西（黃喋）蘇三不要哭（競芳）快樂家庭（王琪）　　華光（一四八〇）下午七時三刻至八時半　　節儉歌（周璐）長期抵抗（黃喋）夜來香（淑珍）雙料情人（競芳）別矣巴黎（周璐）從軍別愛（王琪）光明之路（競芳）雙搖舟（黃喋）（王琪）　　上海歌劇社　　新新（七八〇）下午七時至八時　　花月爭輝（嚴華）小東西（嚴斐）空中音樂（周璇）回憶（徐健）落花流水（徐健）民族之光（周璇）慢牛快馬（嚴斐）祝你晚安（嚴華）　　李樹德（九四〇）下午九時至十時　　好時光（嚴華）勇士凱歌（嚴斐）花生米（周璇）安眠（徐健）鳳求風（徐健）賣花詞（周璇）說愛就愛（嚴華）（嚴斐）漂泊者（嚴華）　　夜鶯藝社　　中華（一一四〇）下午七時一至八時　　夜鶯曲（前奏曲）市上山歌（露茜）娥媚月（曼娜）一封快信（露茜）落花流水（曼娜）瞎子瞎算命（王蝶）賣報歌（顧瑛）妹妹我怪你（秦茵）　　安定（八六〇）下午九時至十時　　木人舞曲（前奏）醉花與酒（曼娜）長生果（露茜）寒衣曲（顧瑛）我的愛人就是你（流朗）（秦茵）春又來（王蝶）摩登戀愛（曼娜）銀色的凄凉（露茜）　　丁香社　　大中華（一一六〇）七時三刻至八時半　　四時吟（雯仙）風雨歸舟（飛虹）心琴曲（琳琍）戀愛明星（飛亞）回憶（變仙）窮富姻綠（飛虹）路柳牆花（琳琍）鐵馬金戈曲（飛亞）　　淸萍社　　航業（二八〇）下午九時三刻至十時半　　一封快信（純美）休息五分鐘（徐琦）路柳牆花（王琪）你要那一個抱（麗影）鐵馬金戈曲（文元）彈詞　　周劍虹大紅袍　　東方（一〇二〇）上午十一時至十二時　　開篇「百壽圖」　　天降麒麟福壽全。壽星騎鹿到堂前。先有壽星來上壽。壽曲唱進壽廳前。壽檯一隻中間擺。左右分開壽臘扦，壽爛浪響描壽字。壽爐裏向壽香姻。壽桃壽糕分左右。一杯壽茶敬壽仙。八把壽椅東西擺。雕刻仙人壽八仙。南極仙翁。騎鹿。隨地行走蔴姑仙。東方湖楚山偷桃喫。沉香刻就鬼谷仙。張仙送子行千里。黎山老母愛修仙。陳搏一聦千年睏。王母娘娘在雲間。百壽圖一幅當中掛。左右分開壽對聯。上一聯福壽壽福添福壽。下一聯是壽福福壽壽千年。壽比南山萬萬年。）　　程方丹李蓮蓀毛家書　　華美（一〇六〇）下午三時至三時三刻　　開篇「吃煠蟹」　　煠蟹蘇州最著名。洋澄湖金爪更歡迎。何至有一蟹不如一蟹嘆。對蟹分兩要滿一斤。可恨他。結連蟹將身强硬。幸虧騙入牢籠一盞燈二從此請君入鍋金錢力。問他可要再橫行。有的是對菊持蟹風雅士。無腸公子常題吟。有的是約到酒家同吃蟹。親朋叙飲甚開心。有的是圓坐合家齋大嚼。尖臍團臍滿盤盛。最可笑吃蟹每把鉗先棄難道怕死蟹還要夾殺人。兒童最喜將鉗剝。配做雙雙蝴蝶形。蟹壳裏仙人個個有。

說這就是秦檜老奸臣。罰他世世代代做蟹人。可愛那　　玉手將餘蟹剝。蟹粉居然滿一盆。或者做饅頭。或者裹餛飩。明朝還可吃一家門。正是煤蟹愈大愈肥碩。故而老蟹滋味最得情。然而須防多吃難消化。蟹爬腸千萬要當心。惟有松江新吃法。蟹斗分開盤內蒸，再加葱　陳紹興。倘把餘湯燒豆腐。鮮味還能勝　精。此外風味別饒是醉蟹。油醬蟹滋味亦津津。可憐死蟹無從揀。雖然蟹理蟹氣像蟹形。無奈蟹脚肉想吃亦難能。電影消息「峨眉山下」後天公映　　「峨眉山下」一片，爲四川黃候，黃令，黃美三姊妹合演之處女作。由名導演家萬籟天導演，定後天起在金城大戲院公映，該片以掙扎在多方壓榨下的黑暗的四川農村爲題材，烘托出雄偉峻抜之峨眉山風景，在國產影片中誠屬別開生面之作，攝製耗費已達三萬，聞該片公映時，並由黃氏三姊妹親自登台合唱四川山歌，足一新滬人耳目云。「大家庭」與「小家庭」之對照　　「大家庭」中有五位兄弟，六個妻子，見女成羣，大大小小，計有十三人之多，當新年除夕之際，全家人互相對拜，每個六磕頭，共有廿餘次之多，後來大家庭分了家，化爲五個小家庭，王獻齋龔稼農孫敏都帶着他們的妻子兒女來到上海，創辦國貨工廠，他們受了都市的薰染，大肆奢華，夜夜浪跡舞塲，孩子們則睡在家中，鬼哭神號，結果王獻齋被債戶們逼得服毒自殺，老婆兒龔稼農因刺激過深，以致於發狂，孫敏被其妻之情人毆傷……在這動亂的時代中，享樂的人們必然地沒落。金縷曲前言  佩佩　　葛蕾絲摩亞的金嗓子，是全世界　迷時刻不志的奇蹟。她帶來電影業從來未有的光榮，更造成她自己峯極的地位，這一位時代　前綫的女藝人，够多麼的榮幸啊！　　她的過去作品「歌后情痴」，已成爲去年最榮譽的歌唱片，而縱起的力作「金縷曲」將　短時間在本埠上映了。　　這消息給予多少望眼欲穿的影迷有甚大的力量，而「金縷曲」戲劇的雰圍氣也非常的豐富，有撼動靈魂的熱戀史，有悅性怡情的歌唱，有曲折纏綿的故事，使人同情，傷心，流淚，這偉大的戲劇，是全世界的禮物。　　一個女郞，從有錢跌人破產的漩渦，一個男人——是溜壑中的幸運兒，兩個人乍合乍離，亦悲亦歡，葛蕾絲摩亞和里奧卡利洛分飾南角，傳神阿堵，妙到毫歎。　　導演維克多許琴格，原是「歌后悄痴」的前任，而且劇本也是他的大作，定能駕里就熟，勝任愉快，有驚人的手法，我們等着她吧。　　一個從舞塲跳上影壇的新人—張新珠　　電通「都會風光」主角「小姨」的始末記  羅根　　現在，快活林的「小姨」差不多是完全成功而立待公映了，但是，他們在過去從開花到結果的過程中，正有着許多件事情値得我們的知道呢。　　首先是角色的配合問題：　　我們知道「小姨」是一個笑聲裏的悲劇，這裏所要的演員是必需能够理會得劇的複雜的空氣而會盡情地表現的，在導演者閔騫的幾度考慮，幾度商洽之後，夏佩珍，英茵，新人羅軍都在他的笑意中訂定了合同，而最後一個周鳳文是　引得起每個人的興奮的。　　又一個是攝影師的問題：　　這一個詼諧的，美麗的，輕鬆的劇本，眞是最需要一個但杜宇先生一樣鎊攝影師來搆成它的畫面的，結果是圓滿的，快活林主人張丙生先生以最大的熱誠商得了但杜宇先生的同意，本片的攝影師就是但先生了。　　第三個是歌曲的問題：　　「小姨」裏要二個動人的情歌，讀者們。說起「情歌」你們也許會想起了幾乎是「專家」的黎錦暉先生罷，是的，黎錦暉先生爲本片製了「花花世界」和「在月下」二個情曲，「在月下」是夏侯珍唱的，「花花世界」則是英茵唱的。　　還有：　　這一件有趣的事可以一提，拍「小姨」　　途撮影塲上死了一個木匠，大家心理作用而　鬼，都不敢上塲工作，是英茵小妲以最大的勇氣粉碎了這沉黑的空氣。　　「小姨」圓滿地得到它的成功了。新時代花絮錄  帆　　大家都覺得滑稽影片不過是笑笑而已，沒有什麼意思，其實這是一種錯誤，滑稽片不過是利用喜劇的形勢，向觀衆顯示它所包含的主題，這主題無疑的與任何形勢的影片是一樣的須要偉大，淸醒促使社會人類走向光明之途的，諸位要看過新時代公司出品的滑稽片「王先生的秘密」和「王先生過年」就知道這話不錯了。該公司編劇曹雪松左明語人，在拍製中的「王先生到農村去」一片劇旨是非常嚴肅的，對於目前的都市恐慌和農村破產有精潔的顯示，而初審　審皆得電檢極佳的獎評，這部有聲的滑稽影片「王先生到農村去」問世之後，對於一般輕視滑　片的人們，一定有不少有益的啟示。出版界　　娛樂週刊第一卷第九期業已出版。內容文字有「北平李麗南下赴港之內幕」「東華會將不參加比賽」「張織雲與任矜蘋决裂之原因」「貂斑華擬做舞女」等數十篇。並有銅圖十餘幀。封面爲陳嘉震氏特攝之「陳燕燕游泳池畔」之浴裝照片。封底爲梁賽珍女士。每期售大洋五分。　　電聲電影圖畫週刋第四卷三十五期已於今日出版。文字如：「裴斯開登被控與人通姦」「鄭正秋追悼會別記」「貂斑華將爲聯華所不容」「吳村男傭人和徐來大姐發生戀愛」等數篇。並有名貴之銅圖甚多。封底面有鄧波兒黎莉莉等之最近照片。每期僅售洋五分。各大書局及書報攤等。均有經售云。　　白雲刊印社出版之均益畫刋，由第五期起篇幅大增，竟達一倍之多，價格仍售二分，其一副嬌小體格大有引人生愛之魔力，故銷數增至五千，明日爲第五期出版期，聞資料較以前格外豐富，但其唯一目的，决不談及政事，專以液輸海外新見聞，及校正社會個人之短篇文字，極有解渴讀者之慾望，圖畫亦均爲名流之作品云。　　千秋出版社出版之春色半月刊第十七期出版，內容豐富，文字趣味，有銅圖照片漫書多幀，定價低廉，零售每冊大洋八分，試閱附郵五分，預定全年二元，另贈蔣芷芬女士繪扇面一張，可加上欵，不取分文云。東西南北  三多　　蠻像胡蝶格「照片明星」貂公斑華，最近要跳出這灰暗的電影圈了，據說是想到蘇州去讀一點書，這消息或許將使「捧貂」朋友終日不歡，及半夜登門求舞者掃興；不過在貂公本身，我想還是「吿老歸鄉」的好，（眞希望她別像「訂婚」一樣的玩快手魔術）那末多的浴裝照片已經不負她到電影圈里來走一遭了！　　吳曉邦陳歌辛將於月之七日假座靜安寺路五七七號美國婦女總會演奏「歌踊之夜」，據陳君言此次公演均爲「古典音樂」，尙祈「識貨者」前往一聆佳音。　　「峨眉山下」將繼「自由神」映於金城，看黃家三姊妹的近日努力練習四川民謠，稱之爲有做上海人「天才」，實在有道理，而况她們在宣傳方面亦是懂得上海人的「生意眼」的。

1935.09.02

Liu Jianxu Assumes Command of the Fourth Route Army; Zhang Xueliang and He Chengjun Preside Over Oath-Taking Ceremony

(Changsha) Liu Jianxu assumed command of the Fourth Route Army on the 1st. Zhang Xueliang, He Chengjun, and He Jian, the three oath-taking supervisors, along with Peng Guojun of the Provincial Party Committee, encouraged him to emulate Hu Linyi, transcending regional boundaries and completing the bandit suppression work. Liu responded, expressing his reverence and acceptance. In the afternoon, Liu hosted a banquet for Zhang and He at the club. They visited Yuelu Mountain briefly. At 6:00 PM, the Party, government, and military held a public banquet at the Tianxin Pavilion. On the morning of the 11th, various sectors held a welcoming assembly for Zhang and He at the Zhongshan Hall. He telegraphed the central government requesting the issuance of 50 million in disaster relief public bonds, with 10 million allocated to Hunan for relief. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

(Changsha) Zhang Xueliang and He Chengjun attended the memorial week at 8:30 AM on the 2nd, and then flew to Wuhan by plane at 10:00 AM. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

The Political Consolidation Committee is Officially Abolished; A Small Number of Staff are Retained to Handle Unfinished Procedures; Wang Kemin Remains at the Committee to Supervise its Operations

(Beiping) The Political Consolidation Committee was officially abolished today. Over 200 internal staff members have been dismissed, with only about 30 staff members retained to expedite the handling of unfinished procedures. Wang Kemin remains at the committee to supervise these matters, which are expected to take another week to complete. Wang previously telegraphed the Executive Yuan requesting that personnel be dispatched to Beiping to take over and finalize all post-closure affairs. The Executive Yuan responded this morning, stating that it has decided to send a special commissioner to Beiping within three days. (1st Day Telegram)

(Beiping) This morning, Shang Zhen convened a meeting at his private residence with Li Peiji, Li Jingrong, He Jihong, Lü Xian, and others to discuss various important provincial matters. As the Political Consolidation Committee has been abolished, Shang intends to personally handle all affairs in Beiping, as many matters need to be addressed. He does not plan to return to Baoding in the short term. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Wang Kemin moved back to his private residence from the Political Consolidation Committee this evening. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Wang Kemin is scheduled to travel to Nanjing in about a week to meet with Wang Jingwei and report on the closure of the Political Consolidation Committee. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

Yin Rugeng Visits Takahashi to Discuss Bandit Suppression in the War Zone; Yin Discusses the Rampant Banditry and Difficulties in Suppression; News Spreads that Li Laobao has been Killed

(Beiping) This morning, Yin Rugeng visited Takahashi, the Japanese military attaché, for discussions. Yin stated that banditry is rampant in the war zone, making suppression extremely difficult. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng visited Wang Kemin last night. This morning at 9:00 AM, he revisited the Foreign Affairs Building to meet with Wang again for discussions. Shortly after 10:00 AM, he met with Shang Zhen to seek instructions on official matters. He is scheduled to leave Beiping tonight or tomorrow morning to return to Tangshan. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng visited Takahashi on the morning of the 1st to discuss bandit suppression in the war zone. He visited Wang Kemin in the afternoon. (1st Day Central News Agency Telegram)

(Tianjin) Fearing Zhang Yantian, the Second Security Brigade returned to Tianjin on the 1st after inspecting special police in Cang County. They are awaiting Yin Rugeng's report before returning to their defense posts. These special police, numbering nearly 1,000, will head east to assist in suppressing bandits along the Great Wall line. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Li Laobao's bandit gang, after fleeing into the Mao Mountains of Santunying, Qian'an, were severely attacked by Zhang Yantian's Security Brigade. Around 9:00 PM on the 28th, Li Laobao himself led a remnant of his bandits in a desperate breakout attempt. Due to the tight encirclement by the police force, many bandits were killed. Li himself was hit by nine bullets and killed. The remaining 300 or so bandits scattered outside the Great Wall. (1st Day)

(Tianjin) Due to unrest caused by bandits, Lulong County is heavily affected. Starting from the 30th, the county government announced the implementation of a village cleansing program, dispatching teams to search for bandits in the countryside. Collective responsibility is being implemented for villagers to prevent concealment. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

Sichuan Bandit Suppression Army Captures Molonggou Yesterday

(Chengdu) After our army recaptured Weiguan on the 27th, they followed and pursued the bandits. On the 29th, they divided their forces into two routes to cross the river and attack the bandits. By noon, both of our routes simultaneously occupied Yingpan Street and Zagunao. The local people have long resented the bandits' ravages. Upon hearing of the arrival of government troops, they gathered along the mountains to assist. Furthermore, Li Shuhua's Brigade engaged in a fierce battle with the bandits at Molonggou for two hours on the 29th, killing dozens of bandits. They repelled the bandits at 1:00 PM and successfully occupied Molonggou. (31st Central News Agency Telegram)

Song Zheyuan Prepares to Assume Office in Beiping

(Beiping) Qin Dechun and Xiao Zhenying went to Tianjin a few days ago to discuss the issue of assuming office with Song Zheyuan. An agreement has largely been reached. It is reported that the cost of the garrison headquarters is only slightly more than 20,000 yuan per month. Apart from establishing a foreign affairs office, the remaining organization will remain largely the same, with no significant changes. Song has received a formal order and is scheduled to come to Beiping before the holidays to coordinate the handover with Wang Shuchang. Qin must wait until Song assumes office before returning to Zhangjiakou to assume his position as Chairman of Chahar. Song is expected to arrive in Beiping around the 13th of this month. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) After Song Zheyuan assumes office as Commander of the Beiping-Tianjin Garrison, the security of Beiping city will continue to be maintained by Feng Zhi'an. Liu Ruming's troops will be transferred to Tianjin to garrison. It is said that the Hebei Provincial Security Department will be abolished, with a Security Command Headquarters to be established in Baoding. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Qin Dechun and Xiao Zhenying are scheduled to return to Beiping from Tianjin on the 2nd. It is not yet certain whether Song Zheyuan will come along. It is reported that after Song assumes office, the security of Tianjin city will also be the responsibility of the 29th Army. One division of the 32nd Army will be transferred to Baoding to protect it. The Tianjin-Gugu Security Command Headquarters will be abolished and reorganized as the Hebei Provincial Security Command Headquarters, to be relocated to Baoding. (1st Day Central News Agency Telegram)

Page 4

British Troops to Hong Kong; Departure Now Halted

(Hong Kong) Hong Kong naval authorities have learned that the dispatch of British troops to Hong Kong has been halted. According to news received today, the troop transport ship "Lancashire," originally scheduled to depart from England for Hong Kong on September 20th, has been cancelled. This is because Europe is preoccupied with multiple affairs, and does not wish to divert its forces to the Far East. (1st Day Reuters Telegram)

Chen Jitang Dispatches Personnel to Sichuan to Meet with Chiang

(Hong Kong) Chen Jitang has dispatched Li Shangyong to enter Sichuan via Hunan to meet with Chiang. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

Xu Kai Oversees the Boat Lock Project

(Qingjiangpu) Xu Kai, Chief Engineer of the Guiding Huai River Committee, arrived in Pu from Beijing by special Fu Ji steamship on the morning of the 1st. He then inspected the Huaiyin boat lock project and the intersection of the Huai River and Yellow River at Yangzhuang. He returned to the city at 5:00 PM and visited Xu Dingkang, the flood control director of the canal area, to discuss flood control matters. He is scheduled to go north along the Central Canal on the morning of the 2nd to inspect the water conditions in Su and Pi provinces in order to determine the future plan for the Yellow River. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

Central Committee Members Will Propose Principles for Amending the Publication Law

(Nanjing) Many Central Committee members have expressed their opinions regarding the Publication Law. Once these opinions are compiled, amendment principles will be proposed and submitted to the Legislative Yuan for reconsideration. The Yuan has also received suggestions from various parties, which the Yuan President has forwarded to the Legal System Committee for reference. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

Mei Lanfang Arrives in Nanjing to Discuss Performing to Aid Disaster Relief

(Nanjing) Mei Lanfang arrived in Nanjing on the morning of the 1st and went directly to the Bank of China on Baixia Road to rest. As the government assisted him during his performance tour in Russia last year, he visited various places around 10:00 AM to express his gratitude. He did not stay in Nanjing for long and immediately returned to Shanghai. The issue of performing a charity drama to aid disaster relief needs to be discussed with the Capital Disaster Relief Fundraising Association before a date for coming to Nanjing can be determined. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Mei Lanfang arrived in Nanjing by train at 7:00 AM on the 1st, accompanied by Zhe Minyi. He reported to the authorities on his overseas trip and discussed performing to aid disaster relief. Many representatives from various organizations welcomed him at the Xiaguan Railway Station. After getting off the train, Mei went to the Bank of China to rest, and then went out to visit guests. He attended a banquet hosted by the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Government at noon. During the banquet, Mei expressed that he already knew about the severe floods in the country while returning home. After arriving in Shanghai, he immediately planned to perform to aid disaster relief. He said that the capital also has a grand initiative, and he will do his best to participate to get more money so that the victims can get more benefits. He hopes that all parties will join in this effort and thanked the victims on behalf of the victims. The Preparatory Committee of the National Academy of Drama and Music is scheduled to hold a welcoming reception on the evening of the 2nd. Mei will stay in Nanjing for one or two days. After all matters are negotiated, he will go to Shanghai and come to Nanjing again to perform when the performance is due. Mei's performance dates in Nanjing have been set from the 11th to the 16th, a total of six days, and the repertoire has also been arranged. (1st Day Central News Agency Telegram)

Memorial Service for Lin Xiang Held in Nanjing

(Nanjing) The memorial service and funeral for Lin Xiang were held jointly at Jinglilu Temple in Nanjing on the morning of the 1st. Chairman Lin sent Lü Chao as a representative to offer sacrifices. All the staff of the Supreme Court, the Examination Yuan, the Selection Committee, and the Ministry of Personnel attended the funeral. From morning to night, there was an endless stream of people. Among the officials who participated were Dai Chuanxian, Huang Musong, Gu Zhenglun, Wei Huai, Chen Daqi, Niu Yongjian, Shi Ying, etc. The ceremony was extremely solemn. The remains will be transported from Nanjing to Beijing on the 8th and temporarily placed outside Liumen, awaiting selection of a date for burial at Lingyanshan. (1st Day Central News Agency Telegram)

Yang Shui Zeng Prepares to Build the Baimao River Embankment

(Nanjing) The Yangshui Association decided to first build the Baimao River top and repair the Liuhe top to prevent river water from backing up into Taihu Lake. The association commissioned Fu Rulin, the director, and Sun Shifu, the chief engineer, to conduct a survey. The construction cost is approximately 200,000 yuan, which has been submitted to the Economic Council for review and approval, and bidding will begin soon. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

Various Agencies Jointly Agreed on the Principles of Rescuing the Cotton Spinning Industry

(Nanjing) The production quantity of the textile industry has declined. Factories in North China have suffered from the dumping of foreign yarn, and sales have plummeted. Most of them have taken closure and reduced work as the final solution. Shandong and Shanxi provinces are still struggling in hardship. It is customary to improve after autumn, but whether this is the case in reality is still difficult to predict. As for the rescue method, the National Economic Commission, the Cotton Industry Control Commission, and the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry have jointly agreed on the principle: 1. The Cotton Industry Control Commission is in charge of improving cotton production; 2. The Ministry of Industry supervises and guides the improvement of spinning industry production; 3. The Ministry of Finance is in charge of tax rate promotion. From the perspective of nature, the Cotton Industry Control Commission and the Ministry of Industry belong to the technical aspect, and the Ministry of Finance belongs to the adjustment aspect, but the rescue method has not yet been discussed. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

Xu Shiying Completes the Report on the Inspection of Floods

(Nanjing) Xu Shiying's draft report on the inspection of floods in Hebei, Shandong, and Henan provinces shows that there are 5.5 million victims in the three provinces, 40,000 square kilometers were flooded, and the loss was 300 million. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

The Executive Yuan Urges Various Ministries and Committees to Submit Work Reports

(Nanjing) With the opening of the Sixth Plenary Session approaching, most of the work reports from various ministries and commissions have not yet been submitted. The Executive Yuan recently ordered that they be submitted before the 8th of this month, and scheduled to convene personnel from various ministries and commissions on the 10th to organize the text and submit it to the Central Secretariat. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

Proposals in the Judicial Conference

(Nanjing) The judicial conference will be held on the 16th at the Examination Yuan. The Judicial Yuan proposes to improve judicial administration, improve the prison system, and clean up backlog cases. The draft has now been completed. It is said that other attending representatives have not yet sent proposals to Beijing. The focus of this conference will be mainly on the Gu case proposed by the Yuan. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

The Qimen Tea Industry Association Asks for the Ban of the Qimen Tea Cooperative

(Nanjing) The Qimen Tea Industry Association asked for the ban of the Qimen Tea Cooperative, and the department in charge of the Ministry of Industry is reviewing it. Whether or not to ban it will be decided after sending personnel to investigate. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

Qingdao Fishery and Salt Experimental Zone is Ready

(Nanjing) The Qingdao Fishery and Salt Experimental Zone is ready. The preparatory committee Chen Tiancai and others submitted the opinions of the phased implementation plan to the Ministry of Industry, and requested to appoint members of the experimental zone committee to establish the committee organization. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee Asks Not to Make Things Difficult for Overseas Chinese Returning to China

(Nanjing) The Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee stated that recently, municipal government public security bureaus at coastal ports have been using the excuse of inspecting overseas Chinese passports and foreign family members, making things difficult. Overseas Chinese have lived abroad for a long time and are not familiar with the national conditions. As soon as they set foot on the country, they are subjected to harsh treatment by customs officials or harassed by the public security bureau's water police. If no guarantor can be found, they are not allowed to disembark, causing hardship on the journey. It is especially pitiful. Moreover, the government has never had a rule to check the passports of overseas Chinese returning to China, nor is there a regulation that overseas Chinese carrying foreign wives must first obtain a certificate of nationality before they are allowed to disembark. It is obvious that the card police and others have overstepped their bounds. It requested the municipal government and public security bureau of each port to give priority to providing convenience to returning overseas Chinese and their family members, and not to make things difficult, in order to comply with the government's care for overseas Chinese. (1st Day Special Dispatch)

Rural Service Areas in Jiangxi Province Have Been Established

(Nanjing) The nine rural service areas planned by the Jingwei Association in Jiangxi Province have been established. Current Commentary: The Problem of Industrial Revival

By Qing

The Chinese Industrial Association held its 8th Congress yesterday. The chairman, Guo Shun, delivered the opening remarks, stating that Chinese industry faces difficulties due to pressure from foreign forces and the decline of the domestic market and the collapse of the rural economy, which has resulted in a situation where there is production but no market. For the revival of domestic industry in the future, the association sincerely hopes that all comrades in the industrial sector will eliminate prejudices and work together. At the same time, the government authorities should also enthusiastically support and reduce the various burdens of the production sector. These words are very appropriate. The revival of domestic industry depends on the development of sales channels, and the two points the association hopes for are prerequisites for developing sales channels.

However, those who talk about the revival of industry and commerce today often believe that to save today's declining industry, it is not enough to only consider the fundamental aspects, as it would be too slow to solve the urgent problem. Therefore, they advocate seeking relief through the monetary problem. Even if this proposition is implemented, what real effect will it have? Please review this point.

The main phenomenon of industrial stagnation is the accumulation of inventory and the tragic fall in prices. This is really due to the weakness of the people's purchasing power. The solution still needs to start with increasing the people's purchasing power, so that accumulated goods can be gradually cleared and financial turnover can be gradually turned flexible. If the needs of the society are completely ignored, and only the production aspect is considered, even if the chips are sufficiently increased due to government assistance, and the factories can start work according to normal regulations, the record of the existence of thin inventory will increase day by day. Factories will inevitably have to stop work as a way out due to environmental constraints. It has been common in the past six months for factories to stop work due to excessive inventory.

As for manufacturers, in order to revitalize current funds, there have been proposals to exchange corporate bonds for financial public bonds. Judging from the government's current financial situation, this method does not seem to be accepted by the authorities. As far as we know, the previous mortgage loans with financial public bonds as the second guarantee were only for three months, and they have been repeatedly urged to pay off the loan, saying that the initial arrangement has long been written off. Now, if you request an exchange with corporate bonds with a longer term, it is tantamount to seeking fish from a tree. Assuming that the exchange problem can be resolved to a considerable extent, it is important to know that the businesses of each company are different, with varying degrees of superiority and inferiority, and the ability to repay debts is different from each other. The repayment procedures for corporate bonds cannot be forced to be the same. If corporate bonds with such conditions are used to exchange financial public bonds, the difficulties in the procedures can also be seen. Even if the exchange is successful, and each company thereby obtains some cash, it will still be difficult to sustain if sales are not smooth, and the burden of interest will instead increase.

From this, it can be seen that if you want to save the domestic industry, if you ignore the issue of production and sales, and only seek to increase the chips, then there will be no effective solution. Please take the silkworm industry as an example. Our government has also issued silk industry public bonds twice for rescue. However, the industry does not improve as usual. When the new silkworm cocoons came out this year, the Shanghai silk factories did not see much enthusiasm to start work. Recently, foreign sales of raw silk have suddenly seen dramatic opportunities. Silk factories have resumed work and are increasing day by day. Although bonds cannot be said to be a sign of the silk industry's revival, however, by analogy, industry and commerce must rely on the development of sales channels in order to achieve the effect of reviving and stimulating decline. The truth is also obvious.

The Third International Promotes Redness; The United States Warns the Soviet Union, Saying that the Future of Friendly Relations between the two countries Depends on whether the Russian side can Keep its Promises

(Washington) The US government today warned Soviet Russia that the future of friendly relations between the two countries will depend entirely on whether Soviet Russia keeps its promise not to interfere in the internal affairs of the United States. This warning was not seen in a public document to Russia, but was announced by Secretary of State Hull in a formal message. Hull stated that because of the Communist International, when the seventh congress was held in Moscow recently, many speakers criticized the United States, so the United States protested to Soviet Russia, but Soviet Russia rejected it. This is clearly disregarding the solemn guarantee, and making the friendship between the two countries suffer a major blow. If the Soviet Russian government still allows those who are keen to scheme and direct the procedures for destroying the American system within its territory, it is tantamount to denying the true guarantee and striking a blow to the relations with the United States. The wording of Soviet Russia's guarantee is clear, so the Soviet Russian government cannot deny the obligation to prevent all activities within its territory that aim to disrupt the social order of the United States, and cannot shirk responsibility by claiming that it is unable to fulfill the guarantee. The authority of the Soviet Russian government is the highest, and its power to control the words and deeds of the people is absolute. Whether the friendship between the two great powers will unfortunately be damaged, and whether the opportunity for cooperation between the two great powers to seek the greatest welfare will unfortunately be destroyed, will depend on the attitude and actions of the Soviet Russian government. According to the previous statement by the Soviet Russian government to the United States, any group that intends to overthrow or forcibly change the American political or social order is not allowed to establish, reside, or operate within Soviet Russia. However, during the Zhuzhu Congress of the Communist International, Changyan was unbridled and made propaganda that was unfavorable to the United States. The US government believed that the purpose of the meeting was greatly contrary to the guarantee of Soviet Russia, so it protested, but was rejected by the Soviet Russian government, so Secretary of State Hull has today's message. (31st Reuters Telegram)

Russian Warships Invade Swedish Territorial Waters; Soviet Union Issues Statement to Deny Rumors

(Moscow) Swedish newspapers reported that when the Soviet Baltic Fleet was exercising, several Soviet warships invaded Swedish territorial waters near Karlskrona, and that a Soviet submarine broke through several fishing grounds in Swedish territorial waters. Tass is now ordered to deny this news, which has been published in Swedish newspapers and other countries' newspapers, because no ship in the Baltic Fleet has sailed into Swedish territorial waters. At the same time, according to the time published in the Swedish newspapers, the Baltic Fleet was never training and exercising tactical operations in the location mentioned in the Swedish newspaper. Therefore, the claim that Soviet warships invaded Swedish territorial waters is completely fictitious. (1st Tass Telegram)

Abyssinia Grants Oil Rights to British and American Companies; Italy is Extremely Indignant; The Strategies of Various Countries Make Italy More Determined to Annex Abyssinia; It Will Not Recognize Its Validity When It Takes It Over in the Future

(London) The news that the Abyssinian government has granted an oil concession to an American company has shocked the political and political circles around the world, and people are afraid that this matter will become a new point of conflict. Yesterday, the Abyssinian King signed an agreement with the African Pioneer Company, registered in Delaware, USA, granting the company mineral oil within an area covering more than half of the entire country for 75 years, including the land bordering Italian Somaliland and the Abyssinian lowlands bordering Eritrea. Rome was shocked by the news and renewed its attacks on Britain.

According to the African Pioneer Company, it was registered by the American Trust Company in Dover, Delaware on June 11, with a capital of 5,000 shares, each share worth 100 US dollars. Its purpose is to exploit oil and seek gems, gold, silver and other minerals such as asphalt. The organizers are Mr. Sheridan, Mr. Williams and Mr. Westrupp of New York. Mr. Rickett, a London financier, handled the negotiations in Abyssinia this time. Mr. Rickett also relied on his efforts to obtain the Iraqi oil concession for the British Petroleum Development Company. His wife is currently living in the Almerz residence. According to the Reuters interviewer, her husband did not tell her the secret of this trip to Abyssinia. She only knew that her husband was handling very important confidential negotiations, which had been going on for several months. Her husband has broad oil interests and often travels to the United States for long periods of time. (1st Reuters Telegram)

(Rome) Regarding the matter of the Abyssinian Church granting oil mining rights to a British and American banking company, the Italian government has not yet received a formal notification. It has ordered the embassy in England to inquire about the news. The British government issued a statement today stating that it is not involved in this matter, which should be due to the embassy in England requesting proof. The entire Italy is deeply indignant about this matter, saying that the area occupied by this concession is in fact half of the entire most fertile area, which is located in the highlands and has always been known for its mineral, water conservancy and natural resources. The amount of kerosene it contains can be comparable to the Mosul area of Iraq. The Italian responsible party believes that the British government claims to have known nothing about such major commercial negotiations beforehand, which is quite surprising. Regardless of the serious nature of this concession, its financial assistance to the Abyssinian Kingdom is an unfriendly action against Italy. In addition, this concession was granted at the last minute, when the situation was at its worst. When this area is taken over by Italy in the future, the Italian government will not recognize its validity. In short, Italy's plan for Abyssinia has been decided, and it will never be changed no matter what. (31st Havas Telegram)

(Rome) The official Italian attitude towards the news of Abyssinia's concession of oil rights differs from the attitude of the newspapers, that is, it does not want to express its opinion. It also said that this news is still a newspaper rumor and is not enough to be used as evidence. However, people here firmly believe that the authorities have instructed the Italian ambassador to England to inquire about everything. If it is true, the Italian government will consider Britain to be in breach of contract and the United States to be undermining its declaration of neutrality. Furthermore, even if Britain and the United States claim that it is a private action, they cannot shirk their responsibility. In short, Abyssinia's concession plan can never change Italy's determination to take action against Abyssinia. (1st National Telegram)

(Paris) A reporter from the Paris Evening Post sent a telegram from the capital of Abyssinia to verify the signing of the oil concession agreement given to an American company. It also said that the Abyssinian king is now undoubtedly seeking to place himself under the economic protection of the Anglo-Saxon countries in order to obtain their assistance. People in the capital of Abyssinia all believe that the Abyssinian king no longer needs to deal with Italy alone, but American circles there believe that this concession may not change the trend of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute. Implementation Begins Yesterday: Spot Checks on Telegraph Bureau Records; Ministry of Communications Orders the Telegraph Administration Bureau to Handle; Disciplinary Action for Delays

A Datong News Agency report states that in order to rectify telegraph administration and prevent delays or advances in official reports and retransmissions, the Ministry of Communications has specially formulated eight articles on spot-checking telegrams and ordered all telegraph bureaus to implement them starting yesterday. The Datong News Agency reporter has extracted them as follows:

Ministry of Communications General Order

Communications Instruction

No. 4065

Regarding whether official reports and retransmissions are irregular, and whether there are advances or delays in transmission, the Ministry has previously issued a general order to all relevant administrations to conduct monthly spot checks on the records of their affiliated bureaus and offices for rectification. Now, in order to standardize the procedures for compliance, a "Spot Check of Telegrams Measures" is hereby specified and issued, which you are to follow. This order includes a copy of the "Spot Check of Telegrams Measures."

Spot Check Measures

(1) Each administration shall, in accordance with the provisions of these measures, conduct monthly spot checks on the incoming, outgoing, retransmitted, and official telegram records of its affiliated bureaus and offices.

(2) Each month, spot checks shall be conducted on the records of at least five bureaus, one day of records per bureau.

(3) The telegram records to be spot-checked shall be limited to those from three months prior.

(4) The following items shall be noted during spot checks of telegram records:

a. Those delayed for an excessive period.

b. Telegrams delayed for more than 15 minutes, with no reason noted on the back of the record.

c. Re-transmissions that were delayed before sending.

d. Illegible handwriting.

e. Paper strips pasted improperly.

f. Misspelled place names for sending or receiving.

g. Errors in telegram type or number of words charged.

h. Inconsistencies in the order of arrival and sending times.

i. Irregular official telegrams.

j. Other items requiring attention in telegram operations.

(5) If any of the items mentioned in the preceding article are found during the spot check, salary deductions or demerits shall be given as disciplinary action, depending on the severity of the circumstances.

(6) After the spot check of telegram records is completed, a list of the following five items shall be compiled: "Name of the Bureau Checked," "Date of Telegrams Checked," "Number of Incoming, Outgoing, Retransmitted, and Official Telegrams," "Results of the Check," and "Disciplinary Actions Taken," together with the relevant copies of the telegram records, and submitted to the Telegraph Administration Department of the Ministry of Communications for review.

(7) The Telegraph Administration Department of the Ministry of Communications may conduct further reviews of the telegram records spot-checked by each administration, if necessary.

(8) These measures shall be implemented starting from September 1, 1935.

Stamp Tax Law and Detailed Rules: Implemented Starting Yesterday; Overseas Chinese and Foreign Merchants Must Comply

A Shenshi News Agency report states that the new Stamp Tax Law was implemented starting yesterday, and all merchants, both overseas Chinese and foreign nationals, must comply. Stamp Tax Supervisory Committee members will also depart for various provinces starting today (the 2nd) to conduct inspections. The details are as follows:

Implementation Begins Yesterday

The new Stamp Tax Law was promulgated by the National Government on December 8, 1934. The National Government ordered the Ministry of Finance to implement it starting on September 1, 1935. After receiving the order, the Ministry of Finance immediately issued a notice to all provinces and cities to comply starting yesterday. At the same time, all previous provisional regulations and implementation rules of various provinces and cities, as well as all approved cases by the Ministry of Finance for exemption, delayed payment, or reduced payment of stamp tax, are also abolished.

Dispatching Personnel for Supervision

In order to rectify national taxes and strictly supervise the handling of stamp tax collection in various provinces and cities, the Ministry of Finance ordered the establishment of a Stamp Tax Inspection Committee under the Tax Affairs Department. Personnel were designated for intensive training, which has now been completed. As the new Stamp Tax Law has been implemented starting yesterday, the inspectors will also begin departing in batches within today and tomorrow for Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, Henan, Shandong, Shaanxi, and other provinces to carry out supervision. The inspectors are Li Yuan, Lin Yuchong, Chen Mengfu, Meng Zhijun, Shen Zhao, Zhang Zhaomin, Qin Zhifu, Kong Qingzhi, Han Lide, Liang Zaoming, Li Chengshun, Cheng Jiyun, Liu Juhe, Li Ziwu, Gu Xianzeng, Li Guoqi, Luo Chunan, Wan Fuda, Liu Hongxi, Zhang Zhaofu, and 20 others.

Foreign Merchants Must Affix Stamps

With the implementation of the new Stamp Tax Law this time, Chinese and foreign merchants must comply equally. In the past, many overseas Chinese merchants from various countries often used treaties as an excuse not to comply with our country's laws and regulations, which was not in accordance with the law. Therefore, before the implementation of the new Stamp Tax Law, the Ministry of Finance had consulted with the embassies of various countries in China through the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to comply with the newly promulgated stamp tax laws and regulations and pay taxes in order to uphold sovereignty. Therefore, starting yesterday, foreign overseas Chinese merchants are also equally obligated to pay taxes.

The China General Chamber of Industry Held a General Meeting Yesterday

Guo Shun, Wang Yunwu, and Others Were Elected as This Year's Committee Members; Important Proposals Such as Equal Treatment for Wheat Flour Unified Tax Were Passed

The China General Federation of Industry convened its eighth general meeting at 10:00 AM yesterday at its headquarters at 115 Hankou Road. He Bingbao, Director of the International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, provided guidance, elected executive committee members, and passed various proposals. The details are as follows:

Members Present

Members present included Guo Shun of Yong'an Textile Company, Hu Xiyuan of China Yabuer Electric Appliance Factory, Zhu Gengtao of Renfeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Liu Jingji of Dacheng Yarn Factory, Yan Qingxiang of Sulun Yarn Factory, Zhou Xinkang of Shengfeng Yarn Factory, Xue Fuji of Dahua Rubber Factory, Cheng Nianpeng of Zhanghua Woolen Mill, Wang Yunwu of Commercial Press (represented by Huang Zhongming), Pu Zhida of Fuxin No. 1 Factory, Xu Guanqun of Xinya Pharmaceutical Factory, Weng Yousan of Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, Wang Xiaoliang of Suzhou Socks Factory, Dafeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Zhentai Yarn Factory, Saixing Yarn Factory Wang Qiyu, Wang Yaochen of Shanghai Flour Association, Sun Binan, Zhang Zemin of Chinese Yarn Factory Federation, Wu Yun first of Tianchu MSG Factory, Yu Xueyang of Tianyuan Electrochemical Factory, Xue Mingjian and Pan Guojun of Jiangsu National Goods Factory Federation, Xu Xiaochu of Sino-French Pharmacy, Cai Shengbai of Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, Li Yanshi and Shen Sifang of China National Private Power Industry Federation, Chengxu of Merlin Canned Food Company, Fang Jiange of Shanghai Enamelware Industry Association, Yang Jingshi of Shanghai Electrical Appliance Manufacturing Industry Association, Lin Yuanmeng representing Jinan Branch, Chengtong Yarn Factory, Renfeng Yarn Factory, Zhan Jingtang of Qingdao Branch, Dai Gengxin of Huacheng Tobacco Company, Lao Jingxiu of Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company, Wang Yinqiao of Jiangsu, Zhejiang and Anhui Inland Flour Association, Wang Boqi of Xinwen Newspaper, Lu Feibo Hong of Zhonghua Book Company, Mo Jingyong representing Suzhou Branch, Suzhou Santai Factory, Yao Xizhou of China Cement Company, and Li Yuncheng of China Industrial Gas Company, totaling more than 80 people.

Chairman's Speech

The presidium consisted of Guo Shun, Hu Xiyuan, and Qian Chengxu, with Wu Shuchen as the recorder. After the formalities, Guo Shun delivered a speech, saying, "Fellow representatives, today is the eighth general meeting of our association. I am extremely pleased that you have taken the time to attend. Our association has been in existence for eight years since its establishment. You are all aware of the process we have gone through. We have been struggling through extremely difficult and arduous times, but fortunately, with the help of the members and the efforts of the committee members, we now have more than 200 members distributed throughout the country. All future work still depends on the focus of the association and joint efforts to achieve final success. The world's production situation is now more complex than in the past, especially in China. On the one hand, we have the invasion of foreign forces, which is difficult to deal with. At the same time, the domestic market is declining and the rural areas are collapsing, making us a country with property but no market, which further intensifies the economic pressure. In order to revive China's industry today and to find ways to break free from the shackles of foreign forces, our association sincerely hopes that all our comrades in the industrial sector can eliminate personal prejudices and work together. At the same time, the government authorities can also provide care and reduce the various burdens on the biological world. As long as the period is slightly longer and the policies and guidelines do not change, the day of revival can be expected. I have served as the chairman of this association for two terms, and I have made very few contributions to the association. I hope you will forgive me." Then, Director He of the Ministry of Industry provided guidance, expressing his hope for the development of the association with very sincere words. Next, the articles of association were amended.

Election of Executive Committee Members

Lunch was served at noon, and Wang Zhisheng, a representative of the International Labour Organization, was welcomed and reported on the situation at the conference. The election began in the afternoon. Guo Shun received 150 votes, Wang Yunwu 146 votes, Hu Xiyuan 145 votes, Cai Shengbai 142 votes, Wu Yun first 141 votes, Qian Chengxu 137 votes, Wang Qiyu 136 votes, Lao Jingxiu 134 votes, Wang Yaochen 134 votes, Lu Feibo Hong 132 votes, Wang Boqi 131 votes, Dai Gengxin 131 votes, Xu Xiaochu 121 votes, Xu Guanqun 101 votes, Cheng Nianpeng 92 votes, Yan Yousan 88 votes, Zhu Gengtao 86 votes, Yan Qingxiang 85 votes, Li Yuncheng 81 votes, Dai Jingtang 76 votes, and Yao Xizhou 73 votes. They were elected as members of this year's committee. In accordance with the provisions of the articles of association, an executive committee will be convened on a regular basis to elect the chairman, committee members, and standing committee members.

Passing of Various Proposals

Finally, the proposals were discussed and passed: (1) The Shanghai Flour Mill Industry Association proposed that the unified tax on wheat flour should be treated equally in order to maintain the flour industry and demonstrate credibility. (2) The Jiangsu National Goods Factory Federation proposed that the central government should, in accordance with Shanghai precedents, promptly allocate 25 million yuan in financial public bonds to assist in the relief of the province's industry. And (3) the association's committee proposed the organization of a tariff research committee to study the current tariff issues in order to contribute to government adoption in the future and other proposals. A formal document will be prepared immediately to request the government to consider implementation in order to realize the facts quickly, and representatives will be sent to Beijing to make suggestions to various central committee members in order to be proposed and passed at the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Committee.

Shanghai Municipal Public Bond Overview

A Central News Agency report states that the Shanghai Municipal Government has successively issued 6 million yuan of Revival Public Bonds and 3.5 million yuan of 1934 Municipal Public Bonds, all of which were underwritten by foreign merchants. After the issuance, they were traded in the Public Concession, which is managed by international personnel. Various circles in Shanghai, both Chinese and foreign, competed to invest, so the price once rose to 3% above par value (that is, 103 yuan per 100 yuan). Recently, trading has been sluggish, and the prices of various stocks and securities have mostly fallen. Even the bonds of the Shanghai Electric Power Company have fallen to around 77 or 78 yuan. These two bonds could not be an exception, but their lowest market price can still be maintained at around 80%. The decline in the price of these bonds is enough to prove the decline in the city's economy and the lack of financial circulation. If the city's economy gradually recovers, the bond price will naturally rise steadily. Recently, the Shanghai Financial and Commercial Newspaper published a detailed overview of Shanghai Municipal Public Bonds. It is translated as follows:

1932 Shanghai Municipal Revival Public Bond

Although the principal and interest of this public bond have been paid on time every time, the market price has still been weak in recent months, falling by 20% from the face value. As of June of this year, in addition to the repayment of principal and interest, there is still a fund of 293,474 yuan, which is more than half of the reserve amount stipulated by the municipal government and the underwriters for the whole year. The total amount of the above 7% public bond is 6 million yuan, which was issued in November 1932 at 80% of the face value. It was sold out quickly, and the price actually rose to 100 yuan. Later, due to the tightening of the city's financial situation, the market price fell to 82 yuan. Calculating interest based on the purchase cost, a net profit of 8.5% can be obtained. If the Shanghai Concession exists for one day, the guarantee fund for this bond will be safe forever. This fund is taken from the dock dues, collected by the Customs, and remitted by the Tax Affairs Department to the HSBC Bank every quarter for the purpose of allocating bond funds. If the donation is insufficient, the Inspector General of Customs will still follow the order of the Ministry of Finance and give priority to allocating funds from the customs duties. Therefore, this public bond is actually guaranteed by the municipal government unconditionally. With this solid guarantee and the monthly increase in funds, and the government will never deliberately lose faith, and the fund will never be lacking. This public bond will be repaid in installments over 20 years, with principal and interest paid twice a year through lottery. From the date of issuance to June of this year, the detailed income situation can be seen in the following table. The gradual decrease in the annual interest rate of the public bond is a natural change. Only 138,000 yuan of funds are required to be allocated each quarter. Now, in order to consolidate the annual fund, the average deposit in each period has reached 161,138 yuan. In theory, investing in this public bond and receiving an official interest rate of 8.5% is actually due to the current loss of faith in the currency or the lack of silver coins, or both. However, it is difficult to predict how long this sluggish phenomenon will continue.

1934 Shanghai Municipal Public Bond

According to recent municipal statistics, the license fees collected for automobiles, motorcycles, bicycles, and pedicabs, as of June 30 of this year, as a fund for repaying the principal and interest of the Shanghai 7% public bond issued last year in sixteen months, actually exceeded the amount to be repaid by more than double. It is found that this public bond was bought at 98 at the time of issuance, and it once rose to 200 yuan, but the current market price has fallen to 80%, which is different from the usual situation. It is probably because the city's financial situation is tight, which has affected the securities that should be profitable. If the economy is abundant and there is confidence, operating this security in all aspects will have its reasons. If purchased at 80%, the profit will exceed 8%. From a financial perspective, this type of investment is not risky. As of June of this year, the principal and interest paid totaled 525,000 yuan. The public bond is divided into twelve draws for repayment, so the amount paid each year is gradually reduced. On the other hand, the vehicle donations collected by the municipal government are increasing year by year, and the development of the urban area is showing a steady upward trend. Zhengda Bank Shareholders Meeting Decides: To Cease Business and Liquidate Starting Yesterday; Wu Guochang, Wang Wenzhi, and Others Appointed as Liquidators; Announcement Made to Claim Deposits and Repay Debts

Zhengda Commercial Savings Bank, after a resolution by the extraordinary general meeting of shareholders, will cease business and liquidate starting yesterday. General Manager Wang Wenzhi, Deputy Manager Tu Hengli, and Lawyer Wu Guochang were appointed as liquidators to announce the claim of deposits and repayment of debts. The details are as follows:

Reorganization Last Year

Zhengda Commercial Savings Bank was founded by Ye Hongying, Wang Yiting, Wang Wenzhi, and others in 1925 with an authorized capital of 250,000 national currency, which was fully paid at once. It was registered with the Ministry of Finance and specialized in all commercial savings bank businesses. The bank's business was quite developed at the beginning, but by the spring of 1932, it announced the cessation of business for liquidation due to the impact of fraud and the Shanghai War. In July 1934, a general meeting of shareholders was convened to resolve that the old shares would be converted into 50,000 yuan, and 200,000 yuan of new shares would be raised. The bank was relocated from the old site on Jiangxi Road to the new building at 25 Tianjin Road, and the directors and supervisors were re-elected for formal resumption of business.

Resolution to Cease Business

The chairman of the board of directors is Sun Bosheng, and the directors are Wang Yiting, Wu Hongshi, Wang Yaochen, Zhu Yanqing, Ding Fangzhen, Wang Wenzhi, Yuan Ziqing, and Chai Zhifang. The supervisors are Peng Xingsheng and Gao Peiliang. The general manager is Wang Wenzhi, and the deputy manager is Tu Hengli. In view of the economic downturn and the difficulty in recovering the loans, the extraordinary general meeting of shareholders on August 25 unanimously resolved to approve the dissolution and declare liquidation, and elected Wu Guochang, Wang Wenzhi, and Tu Hengli as liquidators. A liquidation office was set up at 25 Tianjin Road in the bank to handle liquidation matters immediately.

Announcement of Liquidation

The bank announced liquidation and urged the rights holders to claim deposits and the debtors to repay the debts. Zhengda Bank was approved to be dissolved by a unanimous resolution of the extraordinary general meeting of shareholders on August 25, 1935, and declared liquidation. The board of directors and supervisors were authorized to select liquidators from the shareholders, and it was decided to implement the cessation of business and liquidation starting from September 1, 1935, and to publish the announcement in the newspaper. It was also resolved that all refunds of savings and deposits should be handled by the liquidators in a coordinated manner. Now, Guochang, Wenzhi, and Hengli have been elected as liquidators and took office on this day. In accordance with the above resolutions, the bank will be closed immediately and liquidation will be started. After overall planning, regarding the repayment of savings deposits, it is planned to start with savings, then current accounts, and then fixed-term deposits. At the same time, the manager will find ways to raise cash. It is scheduled to start refunding savings deposits on September 5, current account deposits on September 20, and fixed-term and current account deposits on October 10. It is hoped that all creditors will bring their certificates to report and collect the money within the specified time limits. All debtors are required to repay the principal and interest in full from now on as soon as possible, no later than September 15. It is hoped that all debtors will repay within the time limit to avoid litigation. In addition to the overall board of directors and supervisors reporting to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, and the liquidators reporting to the court for record, this announcement is specially made. Liquidators Wu Guochang, Wang Wenzhi, and Tu Hengli, together.

Refund of Deposits

The Xinsheng News Agency reporter learned from the bank yesterday morning that the reason for the cessation of business and self-liquidation this time was the impact of the economic downturn, and it was difficult to recover the loans. Therefore, all shareholders had no intention of continuing to operate, and it was resolved to dissolve. As for (A) the deposit part, (1) the savings department is about 30,000 yuan, (2) the current deposits are about 40,000 yuan, totaling about 70,000 yuan. (B) the loan part, mortgages, credit, etc. total about 300,000 yuan. Liquidation will be handled immediately, and all depositors' deposits will be refunded in full.

After the Joint Strike of Oil Cake Manufacturers: Over 10,000 Oil Workers Appeal for Relief; Re-telegram to the Central and Southwest Authorities to Abolish the Bran Tax; Will Set Off to Petition After the Hankou Representatives Arrive in Shanghai

A Dagong News Agency report states that after the oil cake and miscellaneous grain manufacturers jointly went on strike to oppose the Guangdong Province's collection of bran surcharges from merchants, the livelihood of over 10,000 oil extraction workers was in a state of panic. They unanimously appealed to the authorities for relief in order to stabilize their jobs. Oil cake manufacturers' associations from various places re-telegraphed the Central Executive Yuan and the Southwest Political Affairs Council to revoke the order to increase the tax. The details are as follows:

Survey of Shut-Down Manufacturers

According to the Dagong News Agency's investigation, the oil cake manufacturers who have jointly shut down and stopped transportation in protest of the tax increase include: (1) In Shanghai, there are nine companies, including Dayou Yuchangji, Dade Xin, Suifeng, Shunyu, Daxinchang, Changde, Lide, and Tongsheng. (2) In Wuxi, there are two companies, Hengde and Runfeng. (3) In Changzhou, there is Xiefeng. (4) In Kunshan, there is Housheng. (5) In Hankou, there are seven companies, including Lifeng, as well as over 40 Guangdong and Shantou merchants stationed in Shanghai.

Over 10,000 Oil Workers in a State of Panic

There are 25 oil extraction factories in China located in Shanghai, Wuxi, Changzhou, Kunshan, Hankou, and other places. Each factory employs an average of 400 oil extraction workers and staff, totaling over 13,000 people. Now, after the oil factories jointly stopped work and transportation in protest of the tax increase, all the oil workers are worried that the dispute will be prolonged and their livelihood will be in a state of panic. The oil workers in Shanghai will hold a meeting within days to decide to petition the authorities, appeal for relief, and cooperate between labor and management to achieve the goal of abolishing the tax. Chen Ziyi, a standing committee member of the Oil Factory Association, told the Dagong News Agency reporter that if the Guangdong Provincial authorities ignore the plight of farmers and businessmen and are blinded by the tax collectors, and insist on levying this surcharge, the factories in this industry will resolutely oppose it, regardless of any sacrifice.

Abolish the Surcharge; Maintain the Existing Rules

The Shanghai Miscellaneous Grain and Oil Cake Industry Association, the Oil Factory Association, and others re-telegraphed the Central Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Finance, Chairman Chiang, the Guangzhou Southwest Political Affairs Committee, the Commander-in-Chief of the First Army Group, the Guangdong Finance Special Envoy's Office, the Guangdong Provincial Party Department, and the Guangdong Provincial Government, stating that the Guangdong tax collectors recently contracted to collect additional fees on bran. Manufacturers, transporters, and related organizations in Guangdong Province have repeatedly requested a stop to this, and the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce has telegraphed the authorities in Beijing and Guangdong, requesting that the original plan be maintained. So far, there has been no effect. Now, it has been confirmed that the tax collectors have decided to start collecting the tax on September 1st, forcing manufacturers in Shanghai, Hankou, Wuxi, Kunshan, and merchants in Guangzhou and Shantou to jointly decide to stop work and transportation. This is truly alarming. How can this be avoided? This move violates the repeated clear orders that fees should not be collected on bran from areas other than the Three Northeastern Provinces, contradicts the authorities' original intention to protect domestic products over the years, hinders the plight of Guangdong's rural areas, and destroys the livelihood of manufacturers and transporters in various places. If the government's orders are ignored and the people's livelihood is harmed, where is the credibility of the country? It is heard that Guangdong Province is vigorously implementing a three-year plan to abolish more than 40 kinds of harsh taxes. Now, the contractors' collection of fees on bran is even more harmful than harsh taxes. How can the wise authorities bear to allow it to be implemented? Therefore, we are jointly telegraphing to sincerely request a quick revocation in order to maintain the existing rules and respect the country's credibility. The Shanghai Miscellaneous Grain and Oil Cake Industry Association, the Oil Factory Association, the Hankou Miscellaneous Grain and Oil Cake Association, the Wuxi, Wujin, and Kunshan Oil Factory Associations, etc., humbly plead.

Appeal for Assistance from All Sectors

In addition to jointly telegraphing the Central and Southwest authorities, the association also sent letters and telegrams to the Guangzhou Chamber of Commerce, the Guangzhou Miscellaneous Grain and Oil Cake Association, the Shantou Chamber of Commerce, the North and South Port Industry Association, and the Shantou Miscellaneous Grain Industry Association, appealing for consideration of their friendship, quick assistance, and joint efforts to achieve the goal of revocation. (The telegram text is the same as above and is omitted.) Oil cake manufacturers from various places will convene a joint meeting after the Hankou representatives arrive in Shanghai to discuss the next steps and set off to petition the central and southwest agencies.

Report on Nursing Schools in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai

The Ministry of Education recently sent medical specialists to inspect nursing schools in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai. The results of the inspection have been reported to the Ministry of Education. The general evaluation and opinions of the inspection are extracted below.

Schools Inspected

In Shanghai: Shanghai Bethel Nursing School, Shanghai Red Cross Nursing School, Shanghai Shangxian Hall Women and Children Nursing School, Shanghai Renji Nursing School, Shanghai Baojiang Hospital Nursing School, Shanghai Ximen Women and Children Hospital, Shanghai Tongde Hospital Nursing School, Shanghai Municipal Hospital Nursing School, Shanghai Tiren Medical Nursing School, Shanghai Zhongde Hospital Midwifery School, Shanghai Dade Hospital Midwifery School, Shanghai Hongen Hospital Nursing School.

In Hangzhou: Hangzhou Puji Hospital, Hangzhou Tongren Surgical Hospital, Hangzhou Guangji Guangyuan Nursing School.

In Changzhou: Changzhou Xinhua Hospital, Changzhou Red Swastika Hospital Nursing School, Changzhou Wujin Hospital Nursing School.

In Zhejiang Province: Nursing School of Zhejiang Provincial Medical and Pharmaceutical Vocational School.

In Suzhou: Suzhou Bo Xi Hospital Nursing School, Suzhou Geng Sheng Hospital Nursing School, Suzhou Gospel Hospital Nursing School, Suzhou Women and Children's Hospital Assistant Training Program.

In Zhenjiang: Zhenjiang Christian Hospital Nursing School, Zhenjiang Hongren Hospital Nursing School.

In Jiangsu Province: Jiangsu Provincial Hospital Nursing School.

In Wuxing: Wu Xing Gospel Hospital Nursing School. A total of 27 schools.

II. Inspection Evaluation

(1) Many schools recruit students mainly to provide nursing services for their own hospitals, which can reduce expenses. Their training purpose is only to meet the needs of their own hospitals. However, the hospitals cannot accommodate all graduates. Other medical and health institutions often express dissatisfaction with the training received by these graduates and are unwilling to hire them. Therefore, many graduates are unemployed.

(2) All schools feel a lack of teachers. Most of the current teachers are physicians or nurses who also hold other positions. They are often too busy with hospital affairs and inevitably neglect teaching. The implementation of moral education in the schools often lacks responsible personnel.

(3) Most of the teaching materials used in the schools do not meet the curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry. Some schools use textbooks, but they are often outdated and unsuitable.

(4) The duration of study varies greatly among the schools inspected. Sixteen schools have a three-and-a-half-year program, two schools have a three-year program, and two schools have a four-year program. There are two reasons for this: 1. To utilize students to serve in the hospital; 2. To believe that nursing work requires long-term experience and practice.

(5) Very few schools provide reference books for students. Even fewer schools have other general books.

(6) All schools lack suitable practice rooms. Students are simply sent to the wards for practice, treating patients as practice objects, which is inevitably dangerous.

(7) Family members are allowed to stay in the special and first-class wards of all hospital schools, resulting in messy and unclean wards. Family members also bring rice and food from home, which may not be hygienic and easily spread diseases, disrupting isolation methods and causing difficulties in management. The reasons for this are: 1. Difficulty in refusing the requests of family members; 2. Hospitals can obtain extra profit and save personnel expenses.

(8) The implementation of training in the schools is mostly similar to an apprenticeship system. The curriculum is mostly related to practice in the hospital. Most schools consider subjects such as civics, Chinese, and sociology unnecessary. Students only study obstetrics theory and observe doctors delivering babies, but they do not have the opportunity to deliver babies themselves.

III. Inspection Opinions

(1) All schools should have practice rooms equipped with all necessary practice tools. Students should only be allowed to practice in the wards after receiving guidance and passing in the practice room.

(2) When enrolling students, all schools must recruit students according to the number of beds available, preferably at a ratio of one to four (i.e., one student can be recruited for every four beds). Because beds cannot always be full, there is a risk of having more students than patients, resulting in a lack of practical experience opportunities.

(3) All schools should follow the curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry and have a uniform three-year program, which should not be arbitrarily changed.

(4) All schools should have dedicated personnel responsible for managing moral education.

(5) All schools should set up libraries or reading rooms, and all relevant nursing publications and other necessary magazines should be available.

(6) All hospital schools should restrict family members from accompanying patients and improve the methods of visiting patients. Family members should not be allowed to replace nurses in caring for patients.

(7) Students in all schools should attend classes and practice according to the prescribed time. The teaching time should not be reduced due to work.

(8) All school funds should be independent to allow for full development.
